

PREFACE 


T HE present volume happens to be the thud one in the new senes of Epigraphy 
Camatica Volumes , it contains the supplementary inscriptions collected m the 
Tumkur District by Mr. R Narasimhachat, between the years 1906 and 1922 
The first two volumes in the series, mi., Epigraphia Camatica Volumes XIV and 
XV containing the texts and transliteration, new and revised, collected m the old 
Mysore Distnct which included the piesent Mandya District and m the Hassan 
District respectively, were published by Dr M H. Knshna in the yea i 1942 
Though the text of the present volume was printed as long back as 1923, further 
progress appears to have been very slow due to vanoos reasons , thus the printing of 
the transliteiation of about 270 inscriptions which the present volume contains has 
taken over seven years to complete As in the previous two volumes, the present 
volume contains only a dynastic table giving in a classified form a very brief 
summary of the contents of the inscriptions published in the place of translations. 

It is hoped to bnng out the lemaimng volumes which ate already overdue 
without father delay with the earnest co-operation of the members of the stall of 
the Department and the authorities of toe Government Branch Press, Mysore. 

Misobe, K. A HILAKANTA SASTRI, 

Dated 86th May MS Dviector of At theology m Mysore
